            <script type="text/javascript">
             // these variables can be configured 
	var travelstartIframeId = 'travelstartIframe-e7784023-3aa5-467d-90d4-7044ced860f2'; 
	var iframeUrl = 'https://www.travelstart.com.ng'; 
	var logMessages = false; 
	var showBanners = false; 
	var affId = '184342'; 
	var affCampaign = 'Default'; 
	var affCurrency = 'Default'; // ZAR / USD / NAD / ... 
	var height = '0px'; 
	var width = '100%'; 
 
	// do not change these 
	var iframe = $('#' + travelstartIframeId); 
	var iframeVersion = '09'; 
	var autoSearch = false; 
	var affiliateIdExist = false;
	var urlParams = {}; 
	var alreadyExist = []; 
	var iframeParams = []; 
	var match,
		pl = /\+/g,  
		search = /([^&amp;=]+)=?([^&amp;]*)/g,
		decode = function (s) { return decodeURIComponent(s.replace(pl, " ")); },
		query  = window.location.search.substring(1);
	while (match = search.exec(query)){ 
		urlParams[decode(match[1])] = decode(match[2]); 
	}				 
	for (var key in urlParams){ 
		if (urlParams.hasOwnProperty(key)){ 
			if (key == 'search' &amp;&amp; urlParams[key] == 'true'){ 
				autoSearch = true; 
			} 
			if(	key == 'affId' || key == 'affid' || key == 'aff_id'){ 
				affiliateIdExist = true ; 
			} 
			iframeParams.push(key + '=' + urlParams[key]); 
			alreadyExist.push(key); 
		}	 
	}		 
  	if(!('show_banners' in alreadyExist)){ 
		iframeParams.push('show_banners=' + showBanners); 
	}		 
	if(!('log' in alreadyExist)){ 
		iframeParams.push('log='  + logMessages); 
	}		 
	if(! affiliateIdExist){ 
		iframeParams.push('affId='  + affId); 
	}		 
	if(!('affCampaign' in alreadyExist)){ 
		iframeParams.push('affCampaign='  + affCampaign); 
	}		 
	if(!('utm_source' in alreadyExist)){ 
		iframeParams.push('utm_source=affiliate'); 
	}		 
	if(!('utm_medium' in alreadyExist)){ 
		iframeParams.push('utm_medium='  + affId); 
	}		 
	if(!('isiframe' in alreadyExist)){ 
		iframeParams.push('isiframe=true'); 
	}		 
	if(!('landing_page' in alreadyExist)){ 
		iframeParams.push('landing_page=false'); 
	}		 
	if (affCurrency.length == 3){ 
		iframeParams.push('currency=' + affCurrency); 
	} 
	if(!('iframeVersion' in alreadyExist)){ 
   	iframeParams.push('iframeVersion='  + iframeVersion);
	}		 
	if(!('host' in alreadyExist)){ 
		iframeParams.push('host=' + window.location.href.split('?')[0]); 
	}		 
	var newIframeUrl = iframeUrl + (autoSearch ? '/search-on-index?search=true' : '/search-on-index?search=false') + '&amp;' + iframeParams.join('&amp;'); 
	iframe.attr('src', newIframeUrl); 
	function setIframeSize(newWidth, newHeight){ 
		iframe.css('width', newWidth); 
		iframe.width(newWidth); 
		iframe.css('height', newHeight); 
		iframe.height(newHeight); 
	} 
	setIframeSize(width, height); 
	$.receiveMessage(function(e, host){ 
		if (logMessages){ 
			$('#logs').text('RECEIVED *** ' + new Date() + ' *** ' + 'message=' + e.data + ' *** iframeUrl=' + newIframeUrl); 
		} 
  	    var dataElements = e.data.split('&amp;'); 
  	    if(dataElements &amp;&amp; dataElements.length === 1) { 
  	       setIframeSize(width, e.data + 'px'); 
  	    } else { 
  	       var elementKey = dataElements[0].split('='); 
  	       var elementValue = dataElements[1].split('='); 
  	       if(elementKey[1] === 'resize') { 
  	          setIframeSize(width, elementValue[1] + 'px'); 
  	       } 
  	       if(elementKey[1] === 'deeplink') { 
  	          window.location.replace(unescape(elementValue[1])); 
  	       } 
  	    } 
   }, iframeUrl);
            </script>

                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Friday, 3 July 2015
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://cmsimg.tallahassee.com/apps/pbcsi.dll/bilde?Site=CD&amp;Date=20120913&amp;Category=FSVIEW5&amp;ArtNo=120913008&amp;Ref=AR&amp;MaxW=640&amp;Border=0&amp;First-Lady-visit-Tallahassee" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="2514055655674577811" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="5863815149870403221" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="5863815149870403221">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/07/breakingmichelle-obama-just-made-racist.html">
                      BREAKING:Michelle Obama Just Made a Racist Speech Attacking White
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5863815149870403221" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://cmsimg.tallahassee.com/apps/pbcsi.dll/bilde?Site=CD&amp;Date=20120913&amp;Category=FSVIEW5&amp;ArtNo=120913008&amp;Ref=AR&amp;MaxW=640&amp;Border=0&amp;First-Lady-visit-Tallahassee" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="212" id="irc_mi" src="http://cmsimg.tallahassee.com/apps/pbcsi.dll/bilde?Site=CD&amp;Date=20120913&amp;Category=FSVIEW5&amp;ArtNo=120913008&amp;Ref=AR&amp;MaxW=640&amp;Border=0&amp;First-Lady-visit-Tallahassee" style="margin-top: 68px;" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     Michelle Obama played the race card again during a speech at the historically black Tuskegee University in Alabama.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The road ahead is not going to be easy for folks like you and me, 
she told the graduating students, because while weve come so far, the 
truth is that those age-old problems are stubborn, and they havent 
fully gone away.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     These age-old problems was of course the racism and oppression 
that Michelle believes white people continue to perpetuate. The first 
lady went on to whine that both she and her husband continue to face 
discrimination as white people question their intelligence, honesty,
 and their love for this country.
                     <br/>
                     The issue here is that people question them because of their many lies.
                     <br/>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="jump-link">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/07/breakingmichelle-obama-just-made-racist.html#more" title="BREAKING:Michelle Obama Just Made a Racist Speech Attacking White">
                      Read more 
                     </a>
                    </div>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/07/texas-governor-signs-important-act-to.html">
                      Texas Governor Signs Important Act To Protect Churches From SCOTUS Gay Marriage Ruling
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-1901090011131230339" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <br/>
                     Republican Governor Greg Abbott of Texas signedinto law a bill 
allowing his states clergy to refuse to officiate marriage ceremonies 
that violate their religious beliefs. Abbott said it is vital that 
religious leaders are secure in knowing that religious freedom is 
beyond governments reach.
                     <br/>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="jump-link">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/07/texas-governor-signs-important-act-to.html#more" title="Texas Governor Signs Important Act To Protect Churches From SCOTUS Gay Marriage Ruling">
                      Read more 
                     </a>
                    </div>

                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Tuesday, 9 June 2015
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://i1.wp.com/delectablemusic.com.ng/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Seyi-Shay.jpg?resize=212%2C320" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="2514055655674577811" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="6390170343213154425" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="6390170343213154425">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/06/heartless-guy-broke-my-heart-seyi-shay.html">
                      Heartless guy broke my heart  Seyi Shay
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-6390170343213154425" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <h1 class="post-title">
                     </h1>
                     <div class="post-byline">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; font-family: 'Open Sans', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 25.9980010986328px; margin-bottom: 1.857em; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                      <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://i1.wp.com/delectablemusic.com.ng/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Seyi-Shay.jpg?resize=212%2C320" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img alt="" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" src="http://i1.wp.com/delectablemusic.com.ng/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Seyi-Shay.jpg?resize=212%2C320"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      A couple of years ago,
                      <b>
                       Deborah Oluwaseyi
                      </b>
                      Joshua aka
                      <b>
                       Seyi Shay
                      </b>
                      became the lead singer for the now defunct pop girl group, From Above, 
which had a recording deal with Sony/Columbia and was managed by Mathew 
Knowles Music World Entertainment, a company owned by
                      <b>
                       Beyonces
                      </b>
                      father.
 In November 2013, the British-born Nigerian singer/songwriter signed an
 endorsement deal with telecommunications company,
                      <b>
                       Etisalat
                      </b>
                      . After successfully releasing a couple of singles including
                      <b>
                      </b>
                      <span style="border: 0px; font-family: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                       <b style="font-style: italic;">
                        Irawo
                       </b>
                       <i>
                        ,
                       </i>
                       <b style="font-style: italic;">
                        Ragga Ragga
                       </b>
                       <i>
                        ,
                       </i>
                       <b>
                        <i>
                         Chairman
                        </i>
                       </b>
                       <i>
                        ,
                       </i>
                      </span>
                      and
                      <em style="border: 0px; font-family: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                       <b>
                        Murda
                       </b>
                       ,
                      </em>
                      featuring
                      <b>
                       Patoranking
                      </b>
                      and
                      <b>
                       Sheydee
                      </b>
                      ,
                      <b>
                       Seyi Shay
                      </b>
                      is now working on her debut
                      <b>
                       album
                      </b>
                      .
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; font-family: 'Open Sans', Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 25.9980010986328px; margin-bottom: 1.857em; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                      In this chat with
                      <em style="border: 0px; font-family: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                       Entertainer,
                      </em>
                      she talks about her career, heartbreak, and celebrity crush among other issues. Excerpts:
                     </div>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="jump-link">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/06/heartless-guy-broke-my-heart-seyi-shay.html#more" title="Heartless guy broke my heart  Seyi Shay">
                      Read more 
                     </a>
                    </div>

                     </h2>
                     <h4 class="post-title">
                      Credit:-delectablemusic.com.ng

                     <h1 class="post-title">
                      <img alt="Toby Grey" class="wp-image-1348 size-large" data-recalc-dims="1" height="379" src="http://i2.wp.com/delectablemusic.com.ng/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Toby_Grey2.jpg?resize=720%2C428" width="640"/>

                     <strong>

                    <meta content="http://e0.365dm.com/15/05/16-9/20/david-de-gea-manchester-united-old-trafford_3298640.jpg?20150515194525" itemprop="image_url"/>

                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/05/david-de-gea-has-not-agreed-terms-with.html">
                      David de Gea has not agreed terms with Real Madrid, according to Sky Sports News
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-3632182606436373928" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <br/>
                     <div class="article__widge-container article__widge-container--edge">
                      <figure class="widge-figure">
                       <div class="auto-size-16/9" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                        <img alt="David de Gea: Where will he be next season?" class="auto-size__target postpone-load--fade-in widge-figure__image" data-src="http://e0.365dm.com/15/05/16-9/20/david-de-gea-manchester-united-old-trafford_3298640.jpg?20150515194525" height="360" src="http://e0.365dm.com/15/05/16-9/20/david-de-gea-manchester-united-old-trafford_3298640.jpg?20150515194525" width="640"/>
                       </div>
                       <div class="widge-figure__body">
                       </div>
                       <div class="widge-figure__text">
                        David de Gea: Where will he be next season?
                       </div>
                      </figure>
                     </div>
                     <div itemprop="description">
                      Manchester United goalkeeper
 David De Gea has not agreed terms with Real Madrid, according to Sky 
Sports News HQ reporter James Cooper.
                     </div>
                     <div itemprop="description">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     Cooper was responding to a story which appeared in a 
Spanish newspaper on Friday, claiming that the United 'keeper is all set
 to return to his native Madrid on long-term deal, and has already met 
with Bernabeu officials.
                     <br/>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="jump-link">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/05/david-de-gea-has-not-agreed-terms-with.html#more" title="David de Gea has not agreed terms with Real Madrid, according to Sky Sports News">
                      Read more 
                     </a>
                    </div>

                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Monday, 2 March 2015
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="https://igcdn-photos-a-a.akamaihd.net/hphotos-ak-xaf1/t51.2885-15/11023173_345625078980592_433519393_n.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="2514055655674577811" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="8328100016586082171" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="8328100016586082171">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/03/kim-k-takes-off-everything-as-she-puts.html">
                      Kim K takes off everything as she puts her German Juice on display in another shoot for love magazine (See Photos)
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8328100016586082171" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <strong>
                      And here we go again, another day into the bodacious life of Kim
 Kardashian.The reality TV star knows No Chill when it comes to giving 
her fans the opportunity to get to know her famous German juice.
                     </strong>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <strong style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img alt="https://igcdn-photos-a-a.akamaihd.net/hphotos-ak-xaf1/t51.2885-15/11023173_345625078980592_433519393_n.jpg" class="shrinkToFit decoded" height="400" src="https://igcdn-photos-a-a.akamaihd.net/hphotos-ak-xaf1/t51.2885-15/11023173_345625078980592_433519393_n.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </strong>
                     </div>
                     The 34-year-old recently took part in a minor photoshoot for LOVE 
Magazine during her short stay in London for the BRIT Awards, a visit to
 Abbey Road Studios and party with Madonna at Mert &amp; Marcuss House 
Of Love bash.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     A photo from the shoot was shared on the fashion magazines Instagram page of Kardashian on Friday, February 27, 2015.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The photo was captioned: Morning! @kimkardashian at the Love fitting with @kegrand.
                     <br/>
                     Looking back over her shoulder in a low-back leotard, the mother-of-one gave a cute smile in the middle of her fitting.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="jump-link">

                      Read more 
                     </a>
                    </div>

                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-894581916999164789" itemprop="description articleBody">

                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     16 year old SS1 student, Abdulateef Asamu  (pictured above) has been 
arrested by the Ogun state Police command for robbing and raping his 
neighbor,  a 52 year old woman at Lambe area of Ajuwon, Ogun state on 
January 18th.

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://www.yourinfo1.blogspot.com/2015/02/tinubu-plans-to-become-president-of.html">
                      Tinubu Plans To Become President Of Nigeria Through The Back Door  PDP
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-1722445736909253731" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="pnl-section" id="africa">
                      <div class="panel-group inner">
                       <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-7 col-lg-7">
                        <div class="row">
                         <div class="col-lg-12">
                          <br/>
                          <a data-mce-href="http://www.channelstv.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/Femi-Fani-Kayode.jpg" href="http://www.channelstv.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/Femi-Fani-Kayode.jpg" style="clear: left; display: inline !important; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                           <img alt="Femi-Fani-Kayode" class=" size-medium wp-image-140515 alignleft" data-mce-src="http://www.channelstv.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/Femi-Fani-Kayode-300x161.jpg" height="161" src="http://www.channelstv.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/Femi-Fani-Kayode-300x161.jpg" width="300"/>
                          </a>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            The Peop
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            les Democratic Party Presidential Campaign Organisation says it has uncov
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                          <em>
                           <strong>
                            ered
 a plan by the national leader of the All Progressives Congress (APC), 
Senator Bola Tinubu, to assume the position of president of Nigeria 
through the back door.
                           </strong>
                          </em>
                          <br/>
                          <img alt="" class="wp-more-tag mce-wp-more" data-mce-placeholder="1" data-mce-resize="false" data-mce-src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-wp-more="more" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" title="Read more..."/>
                         </div>
                         <div class="col-lg-12">
                          <br/>

          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({

            where: document.getElementById("followers-iframe-container"),
            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,

                window.followersIframe.getIframeEl().height = obj.height;
              },

              },

                followersIframeOpen(url);
              }
            }
          });
        }
      });
